A few days later, I was afraid that there would be no room upgrade available, so I called the hotel again to confirm. We were reassured, but when we actually arrived, they were informed that there were no rooms available. We were very disappointed. I was angry. The membership rights were supposed to be enjoyed after repeated confirmation, but in the end I couldn't enjoy them. This made me very angry. After a few arguments, the front desk suddenly said that there were rooms and they had arranged an upgrade for us. We went to the room and looked at the window shape. It was nothing like the deluxe room shown in the picture. The bathroom door and the rain room door were still fighting. It was super small because it was not long before the concert started, so we put down our things and hurried downstairs to wait for the online appointment. msg:As soon as you enter the lobby, it gives people a very comfortable feeling. The lobby is very spacious and there is a tea bar where you can have tea and chat with friends. The front desk staff are very professional, patient, and friendly. The room area is also very large, and there is enough space for children to play. The service staff in the guest rooms have great service attitude, and the delivery speed is also very fast. There are many types of breakfast, and the nutrition is well balanced. There are service staff who guide you to take meals and things, which gives people a feeling of going home. The hotel also has a gym and swimming pool that can be used free of charge, as long as you bring your room card to go, it is very convenient. There is also a Chinese restaurant, Datong cuisine makes people feel the special flavor of Shanxi at a glance. The decoration style of the private rooms is very modern and very affordable. There are shopping malls in the surrounding area, shopping is very convenient, there are bus stops and subway entrances at the door, and it is very convenient to travel. It is very close to the airport and high-speed railway station. It is the first choice for friends on business trips. Very good hotel, perfect!
